LATE DAILY MASS In Sacred Heart Church, at 9:30, 10:30, and 11:30 A.M., Monday through Saturday. Also, at 5:10 P.M., Monday through Friday. 
HOLY COMMUNION Those who are unable to attend Mass are reminded that Holy Com­
munion is distributed until 9:20 A.M. every morning, except Sundays and Holy Days, in Dillon chapel, and between the late daily Masses m Sacred Heart Church.

in Sacred Heart Church and in Stanford-Keenan chapel.

6:00 and 8:30 P.M.
